> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25).** After-hours conductor fire, market CLOSED (18:00 ET; engine YELLOW — only the non-critical stale TV watchdog, both heartbeats/watcher-feed/kill-switches/positions GREEN, both accounts flat). > - **KEY FINDING (stale-breadcrumb corrected — L170/L173/L181 no-closing-handshake family):** the queue item's STEP-1 stated a HARD prerequisite + C11/L180 blocker — *"read exact Saty Pivot Ribbon EMA lengths off the live indicator (NOT in repo)"*. That claim is **STALE**: the spec is canonically **fingerprinted in `backtest/lib/ribbon_config.json`** (fast=13/pivot=20/slow=48/sma=50, all within 5c of live TV, captured 2026-05-07) with `compute_ema_snapshot.py` as the reference impl. So the fallback can reuse the EXACT spec → the same-opportunity-set trap is resolved BY CONSTRUCTION (no live TV re-read, no drift). Corrected the queue note so the next fire doesn't waste a TV read.
> - **SHIPPED (engine-benefit, rail-4 CLEAR — a NEW standalone compute module + tests, ZERO trading-logic/params/orders/heartbeat touch → ships on green tests, no A/B; same class as compute_ema_snapshot.py):** `backtest/lib/ribbon_fallback.py` — source-agnostic `compute_ribbon(closes)` → `RibbonRead` (price, ema_fast/pivot/slow, sma_50, spread_cents, stack ∈ {BULL/BEAR/MIXED/UNKNOWN}). Stack semantics match heartbeat.md exactly (BULL fast>pivot>slow / BEAR fast<pivot<slow). **Fail-closed by design:** too few bars to seed an EMA → stack=UNKNOWN, None values, NO raise (uncertainty = the engine abstains, never trades a misread ribbon). Periods LOADED from ribbon_config.json (not hardcoded → re-fingerprint updates the module). `closes_from_bars()` handles Alpaca/yfinance/CSV key spellings, raises loud on a malformed feed.
> - **GUARDED (the C11/L180 same-decision invariant, in code):** `backtest/tests/test_ribbon_fallback.py` 11/11 — the load-bearing one = a **byte-identical EMA PARITY test** asserting `tv_ema` equals the canonical `compute_ema_snapshot.ema` last value to <1e-9 across all periods, so the TV-down fallback can never silently make a DIFFERENT ribbon decision than live TV. Plus: periods-from-config + fingerprint canary, stack classification, ribbon-width spread, fail-closed-on-short-input, empty-input-no-raise, clean BULL/BEAR stacks, bar extraction, frozen-dataclass immutability.
> - **VALIDATED (paste-real, $0):** 11/11 green; pre-commit safety gate PASS (29 tests + 5 curated suites). Commit **178b6b7** (scoped add — only my 2 files; working tree has unrelated mods per L164). **Bounded honesty:** this is Layer-1a (the correctness-critical COMPUTE core) of the 3-part OPEN-BLINDNESS fix; it does NOT touch the live heartbeat. > - **DIAGNOSED:** the 2026-06-22 fix (307KB→141KB) was a **manual one-off** — there was **no automated retention cap** (grep-confirmed: nothing tests/caps STATUS.md). So it silently regrew in 2 days. A re-violated lesson MUST graduate to a guard (STAGE 4.5 / OP-25), not be hand-consolidated again.
> - **SHIPPED (engine-benefit, rail-4 clear — operational state hygiene + tooling, ZERO trading-logic/params/orders/doctrine change → ships on green tests, no A/B; same class as the watcher_live observability fixes):** `setup/scripts/status_retention.py` — pure-Python, **idempotent, fail-open (L181/OP-25), atomic-write**. Splits STATUS.md on `## [` entry boundaries (newest-first), KEEPS the newest entries that fit a byte budget (default 45KB, safely under the ~25K-token Read cap; min-keep floor), ROLLS the older tail VERBATIM to `STATUS-archive-YYYY-MM.md` (newest roll inserted at top, nothing deleted), with a `--check` mode (exit 2 if over budget) for future wiring.
> - **GRADUATED TO CODE (STAGE 4.5):** `backtest/tests/test_status_retention.py` — **10 cases**: split/preamble, keep-newest-roll-rest, min-keep floor, idempotent-noop-when-within-budget, **verbatim nothing-lost (kept ∪ archive = original)**, second-run idempotence, newest-roll-on-top ordering, fail-open on missing file, --check exit codes. The tool is now a tested operation, never another bespoke manual consolidation.
> - **RAN IT (the loop-closing action, $0):** live STATUS.md **226KB/58 entries → 48KB/13 entries (154 lines, reads whole)**; 45 entries / 814 lines rolled verbatim to `STATUS-archive-2026-06.md` (newest roll at top). Kept window = 06-24 05:42 → 06-22 07:06 (ample recent cross-fire memory).

## [2026-06-24 04:30 ET] conductor: OK — watcher_live TOTAL-DARKNESS class fixed (load_data now degrades on ANY failure, not just FileNotFoundError). The 06-23 zero-rows anomaly's most-likely cause closed + made loud. Commit 57cef40.

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25).** After-hours conductor fire, market CLOSED (engine GREEN — both heartbeats/watcher feed/TV/kill-switches/positions all green; gym detector_verdict GREEN → no detector-touch restriction). ALL author inboxes EMPTY (validator/skill correction-queue 0 rows/lesson .DONE-only/chef). Task-scorer top-3 all blocked for autonomous shipping (EOD-PHASE multi-day fails the bounded rail; SAFE-VIX propose-only params + C22/L122 regime-fragile; CLAUDE-FOLD rail-4). So per priority-6 BRAINSTORM+DRIVE I did the **verify-now-not-later** companion to the 03:36 ET-gate fix: diagnose the 06-23 TOTAL-darkness anomaly NOW rather than wait for it to recur on a future RTH.
> - **DIAGNOSED (the certain second bug — distinct from 03:36's morning-gate bug):** the 03:36 ET-gate fix explains the morning-blindness, but NOT 06-23's *total* darkness (zero diag + obs rows, NumberOfMissedRuns=0 → the task fired and the process crashed). Root cause: `watcher_live.main()` wrapped `ar_runner.load_data` in a **narrow `except FileNotFoundError`**. FileNotFoundError is only raised when no CSV covers the window (the routine morning case, already handled). But `load_data` also calls `pd.read_csv` + `_dedupe_by_timestamp` on a MATCHING file — a corrupt/truncated/empty rolling CSV (a half-finished daily-append; note the diag's recurring "rolling CSV absent" fragility) raises `pd.errors.ParserError`/`EmptyDataError`/`KeyError` instead. Those escaped the narrow except, propagated out of `main()`, and crashed the producer with **ZERO diag rows** — an invisible total-darkness day. Every OTHER early-return in `main()` writes a diag for observability; this one path defeated it. Pure **C7** (silent failure — a too-NARROW except is the inverse of a too-broad one; both lose the signal).
> - **FIXED (engine-benefit, rail-4 clear — observability/robustness in the WATCH_ONLY producer, ZERO trading-logic/P&L/orders change → ships on green tests, no A/B; same class as the 03:36 ET-gate fix + the 00:40 gym-verdict fix):** extracted a pure dependency-injected `_load_with_fallback(load_fn, fallback_fn, …, diag_fn)` helper. ANY load failure now degrades to the history-only path (yfinance top-up then grafts today's bars) AND writes a diag — FileNotFoundError keeps the routine `load_data_fallback_history_only` reason; anything else gets the **alarming `load_data_unexpected_error:{ExcType}`** reason so a corrupt CSV is LOUD, never invisible. `main()` rewired to call it. Even if 06-23's true cause was something else (e.g. machine asleep), this is a strict producer-robustness improvement: a whole class of silent total-darkness is now visible + recoverable, which is exactly what `WATCHER-FEED-REARM-CONFIRM` needs to actually diagnose next time.
> - **GRADUATED TO CODE (STAGE 4.5):** `backtest/tests/test_watcher_live_load_fallback.py` — 7 cases: success writes no diag; FileNotFoundError → routine fallback diag; **5 corrupt-CSV exception types (ParserError/EmptyDataError/KeyError/ValueError/UnicodeDecodeError) each must NOT crash + must write a `load_data_unexpected_error:` diag with the exc type surfaced.** A revert to the narrow except fails loud. **No new lesson minted** (OP-22 anti-bloat — the bug is C7, already a documented theme; the fix+guard IS the encoding, matching the 03:36 fire).
> - **VALIDATED (paste-real, $0 pure-Python):** new 7 + existing RTH-gate 6 = **13 green**; module re-imports clean post-rewire; pre-commit safety gate PASS (29 tests + 5 curated suites). Commit **57cef40** (scoped add — only my 2 files; working tree has unrelated mods per L164).

## [2026-06-22 ~06:30 ET] research: DEAD — event LONG-VEGA #6b KILLED (move under-covers the premium). The 0DTE SPY PREMIUM CLASS is now CLOSED BOTH DIRECTIONS → climb to INSTRUMENT (#7) / compound the one live edge (#1).

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25).** After-hours research fire, market closed, PAPER, $0 pure-Python (re-priced the BANKED wide cache — no new fetch). Ran the LAST premium-vein test: the LONG-vega inverse the short-condor death (#6, entry below) pointed at. The short condor died because realized event moves blow THROUGH the short strikes — so the thesis was that same fat-move distribution should pay a LONG strangle/straddle buyer. **It does NOT. The long side ALSO fails the gate (loses net of full premium) → event IV is two-sided FAIR → the entire 0DTE premium class is exhausted.**
> - **THE TEST:** `backtest/autoresearch/_event_iv_crush_long.py` (flips `_event_iv_crush_reprice.py` long; reuses the wide loader + `_event_iv_crush_precheck.build_event_days()` 46-day list + spot/entry plumbing byte-for-byte; settles TRUE 0DTE intrinsic vs the SPY close; result `_state/event_iv_crush_long.json`). 10:00 ET entry, hold-to-0DTE-expiry, full premium + $0.02/leg slip + $0.65/leg commission, **all 46 event + 46 matched non-event days, ZERO skips** (the wide ATM±$18 band reaches every strike the move travels to — the exact de-bias the narrow ±$5 cache could not give).
> - **(A) LONG STRANGLE (primary, cap-fitting, ~16-delta C+P proxy $0.45/leg): event exp/tr = −$38.82** · n=46 · WR 17.4% · total −$1,785.80 · worst −$142/lot · best +$658 · avg premium paid $94/lot · avg abs move $3.21. NON-EVENT −$67.02/tr.
> - **(B) LONG STRADDLE (reference, ATM C+P): event exp/tr = −$107.09** · WR 30.4% · total −$4,926 · avg premium $423/lot · worst −$709 · best +$1,086. NON-EVENT −$134.45/tr.
> - **THE HONEST READ:** the event move IS systematically bigger than a random day (avg abs move 3.21 vs 2.33; selection_delta **+$28.20/tr** strangle / +$27.36 straddle, both positive) — **but NOT bigger ENOUGH to cover the richer event premium.** Both structures lose money net of premium on BOTH event and non-event days. Long event vol is net-negative — the mirror image of the short side's tail-blowout, exactly what a fairly-priced-IV market predicts.
> - **GATE: positive_net_of_premium = FALSE (the binding fail) → survives = FALSE → DEAD for both.** drop_best2_exp = −$59.85 (removing the 2 biggest winners makes it MORE negative → loss is BROAD, NOT L173-concentrated). **The "beats_null_p95=true" flag is a HARNESS ARTIFACT, not a pass:** n_sample==pool==46 so the bootstrap draws the whole pool every rep → null_p95 collapses onto the non-event mean; "beats" merely restates the +$28 selection delta. The decisive gate is positive-net-of-premium, which fails. (Doctrine queued, see below.)
> - **CAP-FITTING (the structural point holds):** STRANGLE FITS — avg $94/lot, qty6 Safe / qty8 Bold, min-3 cost $281 Safe / $468 Bold, `cap_fits_at_avg=true` both accounts even at worst-day $141/lot. STRADDLE BLOCKED — avg $423/lot → min-3 $1,269 > $600 Safe cap (qty-fit 1 < MIN_CONTRACTS 3 = hard DENY), confirming the prompt's prediction: the cheaper strangle is the ONLY cap-admissible long structure, and it still doesn't pay.

## [2026-06-22 ~05:30 ET] research: DEAD — event-IV-crush #6 KILLED on the wide-band de-bias (the +$32 edge was 100% cache-tail-bias). Premium-selling class CLOSED.

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25).** After-hours research fire, market closed, PAPER, $0 pure-Python (Alpaca historical-options reads only, within the data plan). Ran the DECISIVE de-bias the 04:00 PURSUE entry queued — and it **INVERTS the verdict to DEAD**. The "event edge" was an artifact of the ±$5 cache silently capping the loser tail.
> - **THE GAP (why de-bias was decisive):** the ±$5 OPRA cache (`data/options/`) holds only the 11 near-ATM strikes. A PROPER defined-risk condor needs a ~16-delta short (~$10-18 OTM) + a **$10-wide** long wing — strikes OUTSIDE the ±$5 band, ESPECIALLY on big-move days (the short condor's LOSER days). The narrow cache (a) couldn't place real 16-delta/$10-wide geometry and (b) **clipped the loss on the exact days the move blew through the short** → phantom +$32.15/tr.
> - **THE FETCH (de-bias):** built `backtest/tools/fetch_event_wide_band.py` → pulled the WIDE band (**ATM ±$18/side, $1 grid, calls+puts**) for **46 event days + 46 matched non-event days** into a DEDICATED cache `backtest/data/options_event_wide/` (the ±$5 cache UNTOUCHED). **5,334 / 6,808 contracts with bars (78.3% fill)**; missing 22% = deep-OTM no-trade strikes (expected). Big-move days confirmed reaching ±$18 (e.g. 2026-06-05 priced down to strike 731 vs the ±$5 cache's 732). `partial=false`, all 46 event days fetched.
> - **THE RE-PRICE (real loser tail, proper geometry):** `backtest/autoresearch/_event_iv_crush_reprice.py` — short ~16-delta by premium proxy ($0.45/side, realized %OTM/prem logged), **$10-wide wings**, 10:00 ET, hold-to-0DTE-close, reuses `simulator_credit`+`multileg_structures` (17/17) + `cap_admission`. Loader re-pointed at the wide cache.
>   - **EVENT exp/tr = −$11.38** (was +$32.15 cache-biased) · n=38 · WR 63% · worst trade **−$640/lot** · avg max-defined-loss **$925/lot**.
>   - **NON-EVENT exp/tr = +$9.77** — event days are now WORSE than non-event days (the edge didn't shrink, it FLIPPED SIGN).
>   - **vs random-DAY null (L172, proper geometry, 5×2000 reps):** event sits at the **0.0th percentile** (absolute LEFT/worst tail, not the right), selection_delta **−$21.15**, **boot P(delta≤0)=1.0**. The cache-biased p99/+$13.29 was pure tail-capping.
>   - **By class:** FOMC +$15.13 (n=12) is the only non-negative slice, but NFP **−$49.03** (n=12) and CPI −$1.84 (n=14) sink it; and FOMC alone still loses to the null.
>   - **Tail vs kill-switch:** worst event trade −$640/lot → −$1,920 at Safe q3 (kill −$600) / −$3,201 at Bold q5 (kill −$824); max defined loss −$953/lot → −$2,859 / −$4,765. **Blows the kill-switch even at minimum size.** A real $10-wide condor cannot fit the $2K kill-switch.
> - **GATE:** positive_debiased=**false**, beats_null=**false**, not_L173_concentrated=true, tail_inside_kill=**false**, adequate_n=true(38). **survives=false → VERDICT DEAD.** (The 04:00 entry's own "n=17 is the one real weakness; the wide-band re-test must restore n" was the right call — restoring n + the real tail killed it.)
> - **DOCTRINE (new):** **cache-tail-bias** — a fixed narrow strike band silently TRUNCATES the loss distribution of any short-premium / defined-risk structure on big-move days, manufacturing a phantom edge. The selection-delta being fill-rate-symmetric (37%==37%) did NOT protect the ABSOLUTE magnitude, which is what the cap and the null both judge. Queued to `_lesson-inbox/`. This closes the **premium-selling class** for 0DTE SPY on this data (WP-PS1 randomized strike → no selection alpha; #6 added event-day selection → dead once the real tail is priced).

## [2026-06-21] DTE × STOP-CONSTRUCTION MATRIX (the STOP-DENOMINATOR lever the diagonal disproof named) — VERDICT: **CLEAN_1DTE_UPGRADE. The campaign's FIRST clean shippable improvement to the LIVE money-maker.** A DOLLAR-ANCHORED stop turns WP-8's 1DTE SHARPE_TRADEOFF into a clean win: OOS exp/tr +$36→+$74 (2.03×) AND maxDD IMPROVES −$939→−$880 AND Sortino 14.3→25.7 AND 6/6 posQ AND structural+L173 PASS. The frontier was NOT exhausted — the unexplored lever was the stop CONSTRUCTION, not the structure.

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25). The prior entry below called the structure/expiry frontier EXHAUSTED and named the one untested lever: "the STOP DENOMINATOR (percent-stop scaled to the long-leg premium, or a chart/level-only stop)." That lever was tested as a full DTE × stop matrix — and it WORKED. The 1DTE upgrade on the live `vwap_continuation` edge is now a CLEAN WIN, not a J dollars-vs-Sharpe tradeoff.** SAFE research (Sunday, $0, READ-ONLY — no detector/params/risk_gate/orchestrator/heartbeat/simulator_real edit, no orders). Sim `backtest/autoresearch/_dte_stop_construction.py` (validated; reuses `_dte_expansion_sim` settlement byte-for-byte + the LIVE `_edgehunt_vwap_continuation` detector byte-for-byte). ALL numbers independently confirmed against the raw JSON (C7).
> - **THE LEVER WAS REAL.** Every prior DTE test used the live −8% PERCENT stop. WP-8's maxDD-doubling (−$939 0DTE → −$1,944 1DTE) was ENTIRELY an artifact of applying a fixed PERCENT to the bigger 1DTE premium (median entry premium grows $2.55→$3.57→$4.48 with DTE → a fixed −8% = a bigger DOLLAR loss). **The unexplored dimension was the stop CONSTRUCTION, not the structure.** Tested 4 constructions × {0,1,2}DTE at the live ITM-2 tier, 166 signals, real OPRA fills, 2025-01-02..2026-06-16.
> - **WINNER = b_dollar_anchored @ 1DTE (the ONLY clean-win cell in the 12).** Cap the per-trade DOLLAR loss at **$67.68** (= median per-trade loss on the 85 0DTE −8% losers at ITM-2, calibrated once at 0DTE then applied UNCHANGED at 1DTE) instead of capping the percent: **OOS exp/tr +$36.34 → +$73.91 (+$37.57, 2.03×); OOS total $1,817 → $3,770; maxDD −$939.12 → −$879.84 (BETTER than the 0DTE baseline by $59, not worse); Sortino 14.31 → 25.70 (+80%); worst day −$223.68 → −$67.68 (well inside Safe −$600 / Bold −$835); positive quarters 5/6 → 6/6; structural+L173 PASS.** WR barely moves (42.8% → 41.6%) — the dollar cap trims only the fat-tail stop-outs, NOT the body of winners → it did NOT repeat the diagonal's lift-collapse failure mode.
> - **WHY it works (the core finding):** with the −8% PERCENT stop, maxDD scales with the premium (−$939 → −$1,944 → −$3,008 across DTE) because a fixed percent of a bigger premium is a bigger dollar loss. The dollar-anchored cap holds the dollar loss flat at $67.68 regardless of DTE → 1DTE maxDD collapses BELOW the 0DTE baseline while the gentler-theta dollar-lift survives. **Capping the dollar loss, not the percent, is the lever.**
> - **What did NOT transfer (honesty, C3/L172):** the CHART/LEVEL stop posts a seductive 70.5% WR at 1DTE but is a theta/tail trap — FAILS L173 oos_drop_top5 at EVERY DTE, OOS total collapses to $587 at 1DTE, maxDD −$3,480. Hypothesis "chart-stop becomes viable at 1DTE" REJECTED. The PERCENT-SCALED stop (per-DTE pct holding the median dollar-loss equal to 0DTE: {0:−8%, 1:−5.71%, 2:−4.55%}) is only a PARTIAL — Sortino 18.87 but maxDD +48% > the +25% bar (it caps the MEDIAN dollars, not the right tail). **No 2DTE cell clean-wins under ANY stop** (two overnight sessions reintroduce a gap/settlement tail the per-trade dollar cap can't reach; worst day −$1,140 blows the Bold kill). The clean win is specifically **1DTE + dollar-anchored**.
> - **SHIP STATUS — clears the auto-ship bar, NOT shippable this session.** Per OP-11/OP-22 it clears the auto-ship bar (OOS-positive AND Sortino IMPROVES AND maxDD not-worse AND structural+L173 PASS AND A/B filed) → it ships under the standing profitable-edge authorization with a REVOKE note — NOT a "want me to flip it?" gate. BUT it changes the live STOP CONSTRUCTION (a risk_gate / order-path change) AND the live engine has NO dollar-anchored stop today (only percent + chart/level) → real new wiring, daytime + recency-gated + own adversarial review. Filed as the resolution of **WP-8** (status upgraded SHARPE_TRADEOFF → CLEAN_1DTE_UPGRADE; coupled build-spec: 1DTE expiry + NEW dollar-anchored stop construction, both behind default-OFF per-setup flags).

## [2026-06-21] DEBIT-SPREAD-ify PIVOT — refine the LIVE edges into defined-risk debit verticals to fix the recency drawdown; VERDICT: DEAD / thesis FALSIFIED (the spread can only ADD downside vs the tight −8%-stopped baseline)

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25). The most direct attempt yet at the LIVE problem (the recency drawdown) — and an honest FALSIFICATION.** Diagnosed mechanism: the −8% premium stop whipsaws LONG single-leg calls in the chop regime (9-11/11 recent losers exited EXIT_ALL_PREMIUM_STOP). Thesis: a DEBIT vertical (long near + SHORT a further-OTM strike, same direction) caps premium-at-risk + cuts theta/vega/whipsaw WITHOUT touching the entry signal → risk-adjusted rescue even if capped upside lowers raw EV. **Resolves DIRECTION-BACKLOG #2.**
> - **Built TDD-first, real OPRA fills, $0:** `backtest/lib/simulator_debit.py` (debit = inverse of credit; reuses `simulator_credit.py`'s shared OPRA loader byte-for-byte) — **15/15 unit tests** (realized bounded in [−debit, width−debit] · no-look-ahead entry strictly on the bar AFTER decision · expiry-intrinsic settler exact for call+put · credit-priced geometry SKIPs); **credit suite still 17/17 = no regression** from the shared-loader reuse. Detectors reused byte-for-byte; NO edits to watchers/params/risk_gate/orchestrator/heartbeat.
> - **VERDICT: all 3 target edges = NO.** **#1 `vwap_continuation` (the LIVE edge IN the drawdown, PRIMARY target) = NO_IMPROVEMENT — ZERO of 54 cells improve BOTH book maxDD AND recency-total while OOS-positive.** The auto-picked "best" cell (long ATM / short +$4 OTM) shows higher full exp ($96.14 vs $48.33) + a huge recent total (+$2,232 vs +$408, JSON-verified) **only because `stop_frac=0.99` REMOVES the −8% stop** (exit_hist = 93 PT / **3 STOP** / 20 EOD of 116) + width=$4 lets winners run — "no tight stop + ride wide," NOT the spread capping risk. Its book maxDD = **−$829.8 vs the long baseline −$454.56 (WORSE by $375)**, Sortino **0.31 vs 0.88 (WORSE)** → FAILS L175 on BOTH maxDD + Sortino. **#2 = RISK_REDUCED_LOWER_EV** (maxDD shallower but Sharpe 0.45→0.07 + Sortino 1.06→0.09 collapse + EVERY cell flips OOS-NEGATIVE). **#4 = NO_IMPROVEMENT** (recency bleed AMPLIFIED, all 9 cells deeper maxDD).
> - **MECHANISM (C3, honest root cause):** the live single-leg's shallow maxDD (−$454/−$612) IS a direct consequence of the tight −8% stop (caps each loss ~$39/3-lot). A debit vertical's defined-risk floor (~$326/3-lot) only binds BELOW the −8% stop's floor → against a TIGHTLY-stopped baseline the spread can only ADD downside. The one point in the spread's favor is BUYING-POWER (net debit ~$109/lot vs single-leg premium up to ~$491/3-lot) — a sizing argument, NOT drawdown reduction; on a $-for-$ equity-curve basis the spread is strictly worse here. **The live edge is ALREADY survivable in chop via its tight stop** (recent degraded but NET POSITIVE +$408/+$666, not RED).
> - **No RESCUE_IMPROVEMENT cleared → no live-path/WP work appended. Do NOT ship; keep the long single-leg with the −8% stop.** The lever for recency-rescue is the ENTRY/regime filter or stop calibration (C28), NOT a debit spread. Scorecard: `analysis/recommendations/PIVOT-SPREADIFY-SCORECARD.md`. Harnesses: `backtest/autoresearch/_spreadify_vwap_continuation.py` + `_spreadify_vwap_reclaim.py`; results `analysis/recommendations/spreadify-{vwap_continuation,vwap_reclaim}.json`.
> - **HIGHEST-EV NEXT SELF-DIRECTED PIVOT: DIRECTION-BACKLOG #3 — regime-adaptive STRUCTURE switch.** Both the long-directional book (drawing down in chop) AND the premium-selling pivot point the same way: the missing piece is CLASS-selection by regime, not a per-trade gate (those die by winner-removal, L174) and not the option STRUCTURE on a single edge (just FALSIFIED). Build a PORTFOLIO that SELLS the (mechanical, null-validated) condor sleeve on causally-classified low-vol/range days and BUYS the directional debit/long sleeve on trend days, gated on a causal regime read (VIX level+slope, overnight range/ATR, trend-strength), validated as a BOOK (beats either class alone, no-regression). Why #3 over #4b (wide-OPRA-fetch) / DTE-expansion: #3 is testable on data we already hold (both sleeves' detectors + sims exist), directly attacks the chop-regime drawdown that #2 and the deploy-timing batch just failed to fix by other means, and is the natural child of two consecutive walls (per-trade gating dead + spread-structure dead → the only untried axis is class-switching). #4b and DTE both need a heavy OPRA data-fetch first → queue behind #3.

## [2026-06-21] PREMIUM-SELLING PIVOT — NEW strategy CLASS built + tested (theta KILLS long premium → SELL it); DEAD as a ratifiable edge, IC = LEAD pending a wide-OPRA-band fetch

> **Signal J wakes to (OP-25). The single most important attempted find of the campaign — and an honest WALL.** Self-directed off the C3/L58 structural insight: ~64 long-premium families died because BUYING 0DTE premium pays theta + fights delta. SELLING defined-risk premium INVERTS the theta sign — and should profit in the range/chop regime currently drawing down our bull-directional book. First-ever test of a *selling* CLASS (market-neutral, defined-risk, in-scope 0DTE SPY options).
> - **Built TDD-first, real fills, $0:** `backtest/lib/simulator_credit.py` + `multileg_structures.py` ALONGSIDE the untouched `simulator_real.py` (reuses its OPRA loader + fill conventions byte-for-byte); `test_simulator_credit.py` **17/17 PASS** (both-shorts-OTM nets +credit · breached PCS never worse than max_loss · no-look-ahead entry strictly on the bar AFTER decision · real per-leg cache fills, not synthesized). 900-cell grid (IC/PCS/CCS/IB/BWIC × 180), 365d real OPRA multi-leg fills.
> - **VERDICT: DEAD as a ratifiable edge; IC retained as a LEAD.** **CCS (assigned bear-income): DEAD** (0/150 OOS-positive, best −$4.27/tr, inside the random null). **Iron Fly: DEAD** (full −$2.1/tr, −$1,378 book DD — the steamroller's favorite; "tightest range = highest credit" is exactly its blast radius). **PCS: DEAD** (−$10 to −$14/tr). **IC (neutral OTM condor): LEAD-not-EDGE — clears 7 of 8 gates** (OOS **+$22.95/tr**, 85% WR, posQ 5/6 monthly, drop-worst5 +$21, IS-2025-H1 +$28.96, recency-chop +$8.84) **but FAILS gate 6 — the L172 random-strike null: randomizing the short offset {2,3,4} reproduces & at p95 EXCEEDS (+$26.03) the chosen offset → generic theta, NOT strike selection. Two independent harness passes + two null seedings = same verdict.** Per OP-11/L172 this is the named exception to the standing profitable-edge authorization → **NOT shippable.**
> - **Regime-diversification thesis = PARTIALLY confirmed:** the condor IS positive in the recent chop (the regime hurting the bull book) but does NOT amplify there (+$8.84 < +$23 OOS) AND that chop edge is itself null-positive (generic theta). Premium-selling SURVIVES chop; it does not hand us a *selected* diversifying edge on this data.
> - **Root cause (why the steamroller wins here):** the ±$5 OPRA cache band forces near-ATM (0.6%-OTM) short legs with 6:1 risk:credit narrow $1-2 wings — it CANNOT price the textbook 16-delta / 20-30-wide condor. The benign tail is conditional on the narrow wings (max-loss $100-200/lot); it does NOT generalize to a real ~$3,000-max-loss condor. **Inverse-direction confirmation of C3/L58/L172: selling inverts the theta SIGN but not the L172 test.**
> - **Highest-EV next structural pivot (the only LEAD→EDGE path):** fetch a WIDE, delta-targeted OPRA band (±$15-20 → true 16-delta short + 20-30-wide wing) → re-test the REAL max-loss tail inside the kill-switch → find a SELECTION rule (VIX-character / realized-range / time-regime) that BEATS the random-strike null. | **Bold ITM-2** (#1+#2) | **+$18,784** | **4.70** | -$848 | -$447 | 56.4 | 43.6% |
- The book's risk-adjusted total **EXCEEDS the sum of constituents** — the edges are only partly correlated (Safe-2 daily-P&L corr e1-e2 0.313, e1-e4 0.54, e2-e4 0.076). **#2 and #4 add real diversified Sharpe — this is the quantitative case for shipping them (WP-0).** Every calendar/day-type bucket is net-positive → no routing/abstention improves it → PORTFOLIO_MEASURED (not ROUTING_IMPROVEMENT).
- **HONEST:** ~4.5-4.7 Sharpe is bull-flattered and will compress in chop/bear. maxDD ~-$836/-$848 is the number to size around (within each kill-switch).

### Live-edge improvements: 1 clean (selective) + 1 RISK_UP (J's call)
- **Touch-and-go entry (WP-1) — CLEAN, selective:** matched-day GENUINE_TRIGGER for #1 — **+$23.75/tr OOS** on shared call-days (B7's +$58 was honestly corrected; ~$34 was a different day-set). SELECTIVE refinement only — at BOOK level a whole-swap is worse (fires fewer days), so keep base #1 as the book's entry.
- **TP1 +30%→+75% (WP-4) — MEAN-lift but RISK_UP, do NOT auto-flip:** the +$13.23/tr Safe / +$17.17/tr Bold MEAN lift is real and broad-based, BUT the variance/downside audit (`_b10_exit_variance.py`) returned **RISK_UP both books**: per-trade Sharpe DROPS (0.334→0.322 Safe; 0.407→0.391 Bold), book **maxDD widens ~50% (Safe −$836→−$1,282 ≈ 2.1× the −$600 kill-switch)**, median trade flips negative (59.5% losers). Mechanism: ~87% of the worse trades never reach TP1 → ride to the −8% stop instead of banking the +30% partial = a fatter-right-tail bet, not free EV. **J risk-tradeoff decision; +50% TP1 is the risk-moderated fallback (~half the lift, less variance).** The runner-target knob is separately CONFIRMED dead (L148/C30: fires 0.7%/0.0%).

- **Quarter-Kelly (≈0.107) + min-3 floor, clamped to Rule 6.** v15's nominal contract counts BREACH the per-trade cap at $2K (Safe base-5=34.5%/elite-8=55.2% vs 30%; Bold base-5=64.2%/elite-8=102.8% vs 50%) — caps MUST clip them. ## [2026-06-18] CONTEXT-108: DECISION-LEDGER corruption fixed at the PRODUCER level (WRITE side)

The state-contract test surfaced `decisions.jsonl` (56/122 rows corrupt) and `aggressive/decisions.jsonl` (168/427 corrupt). Root cause = multiple competing producers writing INCOMPATIBLE formats into the same append-only file: pretty-printed multi-line `json.dump(...indent=2)` (the `'Field required'` fragments in the safe ledger), concatenated objects on one physical line with no trailing `\n` (the `'Extra data'`/`'Expecting property name'` rows in the aggressive ledger), and schema drift (`bear_score` vs `bearish_score`, `action` vs `decision`, missing `tick_id`/`date`, literal-string `"position_status":"null"`). Existing rows are IMMUTABLE (untouched); this fixes the WRITERS so every NEW row is clean. Complements the earlier kitchen_daemon `errors='replace'` READ-side fix.

**Canonical writer shipped:** `backtest/lib/ledger.py#append_decision(path, row)` — validates the row against `DecisionRowModel`, serializes compact single-line (`json.dumps(..., separators=(",",":"))`) + `"\n"`, appends utf-8 + flush. One row → one line → always valid, or it raises `StateContractError` and writes NOTHING (fail-closed; a malformed row never reaches disk). Test: `backtest/tests/test_ledger_writer.py` (4 passed) proves clean-write + fail-loud-on-invalid + no-partial-append-on-existing-ledger.

**Canonical schema PINNED:** `action` (NOT `decision`), `bull_score`/`bear_score` (NOT `bearish_score`), required `tick_id`+`date`+`action`. Chosen because the MAJORITY of consumers already index these names: both heartbeat.md templates, `eod_deep/main.py` (CONTEXT-106 fixed it FROM `d["decision"]` TO `d["action"]` — confirming the pin), `pattern_backtest.py`, `near_miss_audit.py`, `shadow_model_eval.py`. = `DecisionRowModel` as it already stood; the writer just enforces it at the boundary.

**Python producer repointed:** `setup/scripts/backfill_decisions.py` (the only Python writer of the canonical `decisions.jsonl`) now calls `append_decision` instead of its ad-hoc `open('a')`+`json.dumps`. Imports verified, py_compile clean, state-contract test still 16/16 green (findings unchanged — no existing data mutated).

**Satellite ledgers intentionally NOT forced through `DecisionRowModel`** (they are DIFFERENT artifacts, not the corrupted canonical ledger, and are already single-line + newline-terminated): `fast-path-decisions.jsonl` (`fast_path_executor.py` — its rows use `decision`/`account`/`decided_at_utc`/`placed`; it reads its OWN ledger back expecting `rec.get("decision")` at L408, so forcing `action`/`tick_id`/`date` would break it) and `shadow-model-decisions.jsonl` (`shadow_model_eval.py` — comparison-scorecard rows with `real_action`/`shadow_action`, not a decision row). Forcing either through the decision contract would REJECT their valid rows — a correctness regression, not a fix.

> **NOTE FOR THE HEARTBEAT-OWNING WAVE (heartbeat.md + aggressive/heartbeat.md — NOT edited here):** the heartbeat PROMPT is the PRIMARY writer of the canonical `decisions.jsonl` (the LLM emits the JSON line literally per the prose template), and is therefore the remaining source of NEW multi-line / concatenated / key-reordered / `"null"`-string drift. When that wave touches the prompt, pin the emitted row to the canonical schema: **single compact line, no trailing-object concatenation, keys `tick_id`(int) + `date`(str) + `action`(str) REQUIRED, scores as `bull_score`/`bear_score`, `position_status` a real JSON `null` (not the string `"null"`)**. Match exactly the shape `append_decision` validates (`DecisionRowModel`). Ideally route the prompt's write through a tiny Python shim that calls `append_decision` so the LLM never hand-serializes JSON. Until then, the writer + contract guard the Python producers; the prompt remains the one un-guarded writer.
